\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Concept Question 0006. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Does ${2 \, x^{2} - 18 \, x + 36}$ have a root in the interval $({2},{5})$?  

\input{Limit-Concept-0006.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{Yes}
\choice{No}
\choice{Inconclusive}
\end{multipleChoice}

What is the reason for this answer?\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{$f({2})<0$ and $f({5})>0$, so $f$ has a root by IVT.}
\choice[correct]{$f({2})>0$ and $f({5})<0$, so $f$ has a root by IVT.}
\choice{$f({2})<0$ and $f({5})<0$, so $f$ does not have a root by IVT.}
\choice{$f({2})>0$ and $f({5})>0$, so $f$ does not have a root by IVT.}
\choice{The answer could not be determined.}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}}%}

Does ${3 \, x^{3} - 21 \, x^{2} + 21 \, x + 45}$ have a root in the interval $({0},{4})$?  

\input{Limit-Concept-0006.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{Yes}
\choice{No}
\choice{Inconclusive}
\end{multipleChoice}

What is the reason for this answer?\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{$f({0})<0$ and $f({4})>0$, so $f$ has a root by IVT.}
\choice[correct]{$f({0})>0$ and $f({4})<0$, so $f$ has a root by IVT.}
\choice{$f({0})<0$ and $f({4})<0$, so $f$ does not have a root by IVT.}
\choice{$f({0})>0$ and $f({4})>0$, so $f$ does not have a root by IVT.}
\choice{The answer could not be determined.}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}}%}

Does ${3 \, x^{2} - 27 \, x + 54}$ have a root in the interval $({2},{5})$?  

\input{Limit-Concept-0006.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{Yes}
\choice{No}
\choice{Inconclusive}
\end{multipleChoice}

What is the reason for this answer?\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{$f({2})<0$ and $f({5})>0$, so $f$ has a root by IVT.}
\choice[correct]{$f({2})>0$ and $f({5})<0$, so $f$ has a root by IVT.}
\choice{$f({2})<0$ and $f({5})<0$, so $f$ does not have a root by IVT.}
\choice{$f({2})>0$ and $f({5})>0$, so $f$ does not have a root by IVT.}
\choice{The answer could not be determined.}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}}%}

Does ${3 \, x^{3} + 33 \, x^{2} + 84 \, x}$ have a root in the interval $({-5},{-1})$?  

\input{Limit-Concept-0006.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{Yes}
\choice{No}
\choice{Inconclusive}
\end{multipleChoice}

What is the reason for this answer?\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{$f({-5})<0$ and $f({-1})>0$, so $f$ has a root by IVT.}
\choice[correct]{$f({-5})>0$ and $f({-1})<0$, so $f$ has a root by IVT.}
\choice{$f({-5})<0$ and $f({-1})<0$, so $f$ does not have a root by IVT.}
\choice{$f({-5})>0$ and $f({-1})>0$, so $f$ does not have a root by IVT.}
\choice{The answer could not be determined.}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}}%}
